    <skos:prefLabel xml:lang="en">
            Ethnic newspapers
        </skos:prefLabel>
    <skos:note>Use specific two-term descriptors that identify the ethnicity of the readership, e.g., African American newspapers, Japanese American newspapers, Chinese Canadian newspapers, etc. One term applies to the readership of the newspaper who identify with a particular ethnicity  (e.g., a publication produced by a Punjabi community would receive the term "Punjabi" rather than "Pakistani" or "East Indian"). Another term applies to the larger culture in which the group resides (e.g., American, Canadian).</skos:note>
